The location is excellent, and the Optics Valley Plaza subway is just outside the door, making travel very convenient. The room is fully equipped with free mini-bars, coffee and tea, and various multifunctional office equipment. The bathtub is large and the shower room is spacious. There is also a dedicated reception area with a lot of space. The bedding in the room is neat and tidy, and the pillows are soft and hard, which is very suitable for people like me who have bad cervical vertebrae. The sleep quality is particularly good. The room is very cool, the hotel breakfast is rich, there are Chinese and Western food and revolving restaurants, and there are many choices. In addition, the hotel also has a gym and a swimming pool. There are few people swimming, and the water quality is very clean! Although there are not many hotel staff and they all look very busy, they are all talking and laughing, and they are very kind. When the children come, they will take the initiative to give small gifts, which makes my children very happy. There are also aquariums and flowers and birds that children like very much in the lobby. It is a place worth checking in, and it is highly recommended.

msg:First there was Ramada, then there was Optics Valley shopping district

When I came to Wuhan in 2005, Optics Valley was still a concept and undeveloped, but Ramada was already a landmark building in the business district.

When I come to Wuhan, I still trust the brand of the old hotel, and there are also surprises

environment:

The status of the hotel boss in Optics Valley is unquestionable. The decoration more than 10 years ago has been very luxurious and advanced, and it is still stable and unconventional.

I booked a double bed room and got a [free] upgraded suite. The room was very large and fully functional. The details of the room are very well done and the experience is particularly good.

facility:

There are several restaurants in the hotel and the environment is very good. Bars and gyms are all available. It should be planned according to foreign-related hotels.

health:

Although the room is large, every corner is thoroughly cleaned, and the public areas are also spotless.

Serve:

From reservation to check-in, room upgrade to return visit after check-out, I was very satisfied.

It is the first choice for business trips, large conferences, family travel, etc.
